，本质浏览器的 ajax&nbsp;</span></span><span leaf="" style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;;font-size: 11pt;letter-spacing: 0pt;background-color: transparent;caret-color: var(--weui-BRAND);">帮你做了这个事情，MCP 的数据通信在 http 和 RPC 的基础上再封装了一层共用抽象。 具体的实现它对底层是开发者透明，但你的后台是传统的服务器，客户端按接口从服务端获取， 底层是&nbsp;</span><span leaf="" style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;;font-size: 11pt;letter-spacing: 0pt;background-color: transparent;caret-color: var(--weui-BRAND);">基于HTTP的Server-Sent Events + json rpc 通信。</span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">如果对应进程，比如cluade desktop &nbsp;调用有道词典，那有道词典作为服务的提供数据，客户端就走进程通信（不同的语言的 sdk 实现不一样，但基本是跨平台的，你不用关注兼容问题）。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">现在你理解了Transport实现本质上就是个传输管道， 你完全可以用HTTPS 替代和后台通信，或者在客户端开发用来做进程通信都可以。 只是MCP封装了更多的标准。比如协商标准，数据获取标准 。你有没有发现，这和我们平时理解的"AI"一点关系都没有？对，它就是个纯通信组件。它是通信协议，不是 AI 具体实现。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">我举个例子，假设我们要实现一个在线记事本的前后端通信，MCP完全可以胜任，不需要和 AI 挂钩。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang leaf=""><br></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">&nbsp;task</span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#9A6E3A;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">:</span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#669900;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">"排序算法"</span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#999999;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">,</span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">&nbsp;language</span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#669900;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">"Python"</span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#999999;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">}</span></span><span leaf=""><br></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#999999;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">});</span></span><span leaf=""><br></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Monaco;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p><span leaf="">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span><span leaf=""><br></span></code></pre><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">对，就是这么多。也就我们把 http 协议替代成 MCP 协议，最终即完成接入。没有 mcp 之前，我们会通过 http 进行前后端通信，拿到自己的数据，然后再给大模型使用。替换成 mcp 后，其他逻辑仍然不需要变化。但你需要引入MCP整个SDK，理解它的概念模型，基于它做会话建立、调用、处理它的错误格式，还要适应它的类型系统，然后不断 debug 调基础的东西。对于简单应用，这可能是杀鸡用牛刀。具体不恰当的例子，有点做一个简单的列表页，从前端用 GraphQL 去调用 后台操作数据库，而不是用 HTTP，最终引入太多复杂性。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">基于 mcp 协议拿到数据以后，客户端要做什么事情，和 mcp 无关，mcp不定义这个。那我们为什么要接入它？</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这个问题很好。基于 http 的背景下，每个后台返回的接口格式不一样，客户端和服务端需要“联调”，并专门写数据解析逻辑。而 MCP 定义了这部分接口组成的规范，为什么我们类比 REST，而不是接口本身，因为 REST 定义了post 就是修改数据，delete 方法就是删除数据等行为，大家按这个约定进行。同样 MCP 定义了 tools 是获取工具，prompt 获取提示词。这样大家约定 tools 拿到工具，按统一的方法解析就行。有没有可能某个服务基于 MCP 暴露接口但不遵守规范？完全可以，在那种尝试定义私域生态协议，比如小程序之基于 HTML5。只要某个平台拥有足够的话语权，那生态的协议自然</span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;;font-size: 11pt;letter-spacing: 0pt;background-color: transparent;caret-color: var(--weui-BRAND);">归它掌控。</span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><br></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="" ></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><h3 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">MCP适合哪些场景？</span></span></h3><h3 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></h3><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">从源码和设计来看，MCP适合以下场景：</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">1. 你在构建一个需要扩展的平台，希望第三方开发者能为你的平台提供工具，或者你是第三方开发者想为平台提供 AI 工具。比如 Claude Desktop想让其他公司为它开发插件； 比如有道词典 AI 能力（我真的不知道他们有没有提供）想同时 被 cursor 和&nbsp;</span><span leaf="">Claude Desktop使用。<span textstyle="" style="font-weight: bold;">这就是 MCP 最大的价值。</span></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">（最近微信也开始支持 MCP 以进入平台生态）</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">2. 你需要在多种环境中复用同一套工具。 比如同一组工具需要在网页版、桌面版和移动版中使用。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这种</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">情况</span></span><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">协议</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">。通常这种工具是不会暴露给第三方用的，比如 cursor 的核心能力。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">3. 简单的一次性集成。如果你只需要调用几个工具API，直接用HTTP请求可能更简单明了。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">内部 Agent 只有需要吸引跨部门开发工具进入才有意义，如果评估是内部自己人，一年下来就几个确定的工具，那 MCP 无意义，会增加调试和开发负担。市面上很多客户端内部Agent实现，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，比如 cursor 、github copilot 等实现策略是，<span textstyle="" style="font-weight: bold;">自己的核心 Agent 调用（文件打开、搜索等工具）特别优化实现， 而非核心的外部工具（搜索数据库等），暴露标准 MCP 接口。</span></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><h3 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">市场上几种常见的MCP误解</span></span></h3><h3 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></h3><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">很多文章把MCP描述为"AI的USB接口"或"Function Calling的升级版"，这些都是对MCP的误解。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang "AI的USB接口"：</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang leaf="">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang ><span leaf="">数据</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">后</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" Calling</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span ><span leaf="">Function Calling</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang ><span leaf="">USB</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang Function Calling 兼容还不太好）</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">2. "Function Calling的升级版"：前面已经提到 Function Calling 是大模型的一种能力，让模型能够以结构化方式输出函数调用。而MCP是一种通信协议，两者不在一个层次上。虽然MCP的Tools 概念接口与Function Calling类似，但它们解决的是不同问题。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">MCP</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">数据</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">给</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">到</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">客户端</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">最终</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">是</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">用</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">Function Calling</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">去</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">调用</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">大模型</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">两个</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">是</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">不同</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">层面</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的描述。（有好几篇流量挺大所谓的科普文把 MCP 当成是&nbsp;</span><span leaf="">Function Calling替代...囧... ）</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;text-indent:-16.8pt;margin-left:16.8pt;margin-right:0pt;mso-list:l9 level1;"><span style=""><span leaf="">&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-list:Ignore;"><span leaf="">3.&nbsp;</span></span></span><span leaf="">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">"万能的Agent框架"：有些文章把MCP描述为一种全能的Agent框架，这就更扯了（很怀疑这些文章都是 AI 吐出来，再加工的，都没有看MCP 官方文档...）。MCP只定义了通信标准，不包含Agent的核心逻辑，如决策、规划、记忆等。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><h2 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></h2><h2 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">结</span></span></h2><h2 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></h2><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">MCP只是一个通信协议，不是AI的救世主。它可能对某些场景有价值（平台生态，工具扩展），但对其他场景可能是不必要的复杂性。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><section><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">开发内部&nbsp;</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">Agent</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">&nbsp;过程</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，一般</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">通信</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">标准是</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">工作量很少的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">部分</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">。我们大部分工作是在提示工程，Agent 规划、记忆等。</span></span></section><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">希望这篇文章能帮你看清MCP的真面目，做出明智的技术决策，不要花在浪费时间的事情上。 如果你正在构建平台或生态系统，MCP可能是个好选择；如果你只是开发一个特定用途的Agent，简单的HTTP API可能已经足够了。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span leaf=""><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SDK源码的深入分析，旨在从技术角度揭示MCP的真实面貌，而非跟随市场炒作。如有不同见解，欢迎讨论。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span
